Our <a href="https://about.gitlab.com/company/mission" data-ga-name="company mission" data-ga-location="body">mission</a> makes it clear that we believe in a world where everyone can contribute. We make that possible at GitLab by running <a href="https://about.gitlab.com/handbook/using-gitlab-at-gitlab/" data-ga-name="handbook - using gitlab at gitlab" data-ga-location="body">our operations</a> on our product and staying aligned with <a href="https://about.gitlab.com/handbook/values/" data-ga-name="our values" data-ga-location="body">our values</a>.</p>
<p>We strive to create a transparent environment where all team members around the world feel that their voices are heard and welcomed. We also aim to be a place where people can show up as their full selves each day and contribute their best.</p>
